Get the bus operating mode.\mbox{[}get\mbox{]}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & communication interface handler. Use NULL to ignore this interface.(ptr) \\
\hline
{\em aux\+\_\+ctx} & auxiliary communication interface handler. Use NULL to ignore this interface.(ptr) \\
\hline
{\em val} & retrieves the bus operating mode for both the main and the auxiliary interface.(ptr) \\

Configures the bus operating mode.\mbox{[}set\mbox{]}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & communication interface handler. Use NULL to ignore this interface.(ptr) \\
\hline
{\em aux\+\_\+ctx} & auxiliary communication interface handler. Use NULL to ignore this interface.(ptr) \\
\hline
{\em val} & configures the bus operating mode for both the main and the auxiliary interface. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Sensor conversion parameters selection.\mbox{[}set\mbox{]}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & communication interface handler. Use NULL to ignore this interface.(ptr) \\
\hline
{\em aux\+\_\+ctx} & auxiliary communication interface handler. Use NULL to ignore this interface.(ptr) \\
\hline
{\em val} & set the sensor conversion parameters by checking the constraints of the device.(ptr) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em interface} & status (MANDATORY\+: return 0 -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} no Error) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\em ctx} & communication interface handler. Use NULL to ignore this interface.(ptr) \\
\hline
{\em aux\+\_\+ctx} & auxiliary communication interface handler. Use NULL to ignore this interface.(ptr) \\
\hline
{\em val} & the signals to route on int2 pin. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}

\hline
